### queue-operation

嬉遊部は自由なパートですが、どのような生成メカニズムを取っているのかざっとまとめて教えてください。

## User Message #2088



## Assistant Message #2089



### queue-operation

そのプロセスを抽象化して表現できますか。

## User Message #2092



## Assistant Message #2093



### queue-operation

最初の音素材はフーガでは通常、主題を切り取ったり加工したりして作りますよね。和声解釈とは、そのテーマの高さをその調のダイアトニック上で、上げ下げするのですが、テーマに由来することもありますよね。そして嬉遊部の中で転調をどうするかですよね。さらには対旋律にテーマとの関連などのような制限をつけるかということもあると思います。

## User Message #2096



## Assistant Message #2097



### queue-operation

ここはのちの機械学習のことを考えると、それらしく聞こえるように中身をガチガチに手で組むべきではないと思います。あくまでも汎用の構造を用意して機械学習の成果をすんなり載せることができるような仕組みを作るべきではないかと思いますが、自由なご意見をください。

## User Message #2100



## Assistant Message #2101



### queue-operation

嬉遊部に始まりと終わりがあってそこには調があるということに変わりはないでしょうから、良いと思います、中の転調のプロセスも中身はどんなものであれ、バッハの曲の解析に適用できないということはないでしょう。複調とか無調はないでしょうから。

## User Message #2104



## Assistant Message #2105



### queue-operation

お願いします。

### queue-operation

## User Message #2601



## Assistant Message #2602



### queue-operation

私も過去にいろんなデータを見ていますが、みんな結構自己流で悩ましいですね。大抵はMIDIの知識が低すぎるのでしょう。あるいは自分の環境で出てくる音だけしか関心ないとか。チャネルもトラックも一緒のものはどうしょうもないですよ。バッハは声部が交差するのは珍しくないし。理想論をいうと使わない方がいいでしょう。しかし無理やりやっても結果オーライの可能性は否定できませんので、それでML モデル設計に進むのはいかがでしょう。ダメなら最初はフーガの技法と音楽の捧げ物だけにするとか。

## User Message #2605



## Assistant Message #2606



### queue-operation

はい、お願いします。

### queue-operation

ネットワーク制限は私が変えられますか？
前拍の代表音が次の拍まで持続しているか確認していなかったーこれはあり得ない仕様です。
そもそも非和声音の取り扱いに問題はありませんか？

## User Message #3513



## Assistant Message #3514



## Assistant Message #3515



## User Message #3516

## Assistant Message #3534



## Assistant Message #3535



## User Message #3536



## Assistant Message #3537



## Assistant Message #3538



## User Message #3539



## Assistant Message #3540



### queue-operation

「声部自体が次拍まで途切れていないか」は、「各声部は単音」が保証されてなければ意味がありません。対位法では大丈夫に思えますが、和声チェッカーとしては危うい仕様です。
非和声音も拍頭でなければ何でもありではありません。教科書では詳細な定義は？

## User Message #3543



## Assistant Message #3544



## Assistant Message #3545



## Assistant Message #3546



## User Message #3547



## Assistant Message #3548



## User Message #3549



## Assistant Message #3550



## User Message #3551



## Assistant Message #3552



## User Message #3553



## Assistant Message #3554



## Assistant Message #3555



## User Message #3556



## Assistant Message #3557



## User Message #3558



## Assistant Message #3559



## Assistant Message #3560



## User Message #3561



## Assistant Message #3562



## User Message #3563



## Assistant Message #3564



### queue-operation

「代表音」を推測で選ぶ方法は、人間の聴覚に反します。それに基けば些細なミスは全部許されます。八分音符を全部非和声音として処理すると、非常に緩い曲に聞こえるでしょう。誰の耳にも装飾音や經過音として聞かれる部分以外は、和声的配慮をするべきでしょう。聴感上も威厳を醸し出して好ましいので実際にそのような曲も多いと思います。

## Assistant Message #3568

## User Message #3570

### queue-operation

転調は無秩序と呼んでいいレベルですね。転調については古典和声学に用例として認められた方法を遵守するのが必要でしょう。それでも十分多様性があります。たとえ近親調へとはいえカデンツの流れを無視して転調を繰り返すと現代音楽なって当然かと思います。

### queue-operation

### queue-operation

嬉遊部は自由な形式なので機械学習に任せるのが基本でしょうが、バッハの和声進行や転調がちゃんと拾えているのか気がかりです。

### queue-operation

まあ、そうかもしれませんが、和声学の基本をカバーできなければ先に進んでも意味ありませんよね。非和声音のフィルタリングも安直に使用されることを懸念します。一部、前にも書きましたが修飾的な部分以外は全て和声音として扱った方がより精緻ですし、強拍に限定するのではなくむしろある拍の中で非和声音を含まない、あるいは展開形にならない形を選ぶなど、より聴感覚に沿った妥当な選択をできるように配慮すべきだと思います。転調判定に関しても不自然な侵攻の場合にはフォールバックするなどの人間的で階層的な仕組みが必要だと思います。

### queue-operation

ダイアトニックに制限するのはうまくいくでしょうが少しいきすぎかと。確かにダイアトニックに限定して仕舞えば、V->IV以外さえなければ理論的にはカデンツに無理やり当てはめることもできるでしょうが、極端に短い長さでダイアトニックを並べても、代理和音だらけでは人間の耳にはカデンツが聞き取れず、結果、調の判別すらできず、奇妙な和音の羅列に聞こえるのだと思います。転調は基本的な構成の段階で決定されるのが普通で、そうすると現在のような矢継ぎ早な転調はまず常識的にあり得なくなると思います。

### queue-operation

一旦修正したはずの不適切な省略が復活してしまったのは衝撃的です。
根音と第三音省略はレッドカードの「不良」です。
適切な選択肢がない場合は、必ずフォールバックするようにしてください。
次は慎重に8分音符を戻しましよう。しかしこれを非和声音として扱うのは不適切です。和声音として扱いましょう。
不適切な連結しかない場合には、他のパートの音も同時に変更して局所的に代理和音を使うのが適切かと思います。
非和声的な経過音として扱うのは16分音符以下としましょう。

### queue-operation

和声的にはなんとか破綻はないのですが、何か変だと感じます。原因は8分音符が和声内にとどまって分散和音的に使われているからだと思います。経過音をとして扱うのは駄目というのは、和声的に適当にスルーしては駄目ということで、かといって、まったく順次進行しないとフーガらしくありません。

### queue-operation

### queue-operation

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Analysis:
Let me chronologically analyze the conversation, which continues from a previous session about a Bach-style fugue generator.

**Session start**: This session continues from a compacted conversation. The summary covers extensive prior work on chord plan integration, voice-aware chord estimation, and classical harmony-based modulation.

**Task 1: C5 removal and C3 strengthening**
The user's last request before compaction was "いや、C5は一旦止めてみましょう" (let's try removing C5). The pending tasks were:
1. Remove C5 from CONSTRAINTS.md
2. Strengthen C3 in implementation (individual root/third guarantee)
3. Update test_constraints.py
4. Run regression tests

I proceeded to:
1. Updated CONSTRAINTS.md - marked C5 as suspended (一時停止)
2. Strengthened C3 test in test_constraints.py to check individual root/third presence (not just simultaneous absence)
3. The `_verify_and_repair_chord_coverage()` already checked individually

**C3 test failures and repair function enhancement:**
Running tests revealed 10 violations where root or third was individually missing. I made several rounds of fixes:

1. Added step (3) fallback: chord reassignment from all diatonic chords - reduced to 6 violations
2. Fixed `_get_diatonic_chord_for_beat` to use local key's diatonic chords (not just main key) - added `diatonic_chords` parameter to repair function
3. Added step (3b): combined chord reassignment + voice modification
4. Fixed duplicate PC detection: when multiple voices play the same pitch class, one can be modified even if it provides root/third
5. Fixed the test methodology: changed from "note starts at beat head" to "note sounding at beat head" (crucial fix - 8th notes sustaining through beat boundaries were being missed)

After all fixes: all 9 tests PASS, 0 errors in generation.

**Task 2: Art of Fugue subject generation**
User asked: "テーマを「フーガの技法」の基本主題にして生成できますか?"

I created generate_art_of_fugue.py with the BWV 1080 subject. Initially used uniform quarter notes (all Pitch objects).

**User correction on rhythm:**
User: "リズムが違いますね。冒頭から、二分音符五つ、四分音符二つ、付点二分音符一つ、八分音符三つです。"

I asked about the final D note - user said "含めない" (don't include it).

This led to NoteEvent-based subject definition:
- 5 half notes (D, A, F, D, C#): duration=8 each
- 2 quarter notes (D, E): duration=4 each
- 1 dotted half (F): duration=12
- 3 eighth notes (G, F, E): duration=2 each
- Total: 66 subbeats = 17 beats (ceiling division)

**Multiple fixes needed for NoteEvent support:**

1. `Subject.get_length()`: Changed from floor to ceiling division `(sb + 3) // 4`
2. `_extract_beat_head_pcs()`: CRITICAL BUG - only captured notes starting ON beat boundaries, missing beats within long notes. Fixed to capture all beat boundaries within each note's span.
3. DP `_check_hard()`: Added None checks for fixed voices
4. DP `_score_transition()`: Added None checks in two places (motion scoring and chromatic clash)

**User correction on pitches:**
User: "今度は主題が全然違ってますよ!聞くには面白いですが。"

I had A3(57) → F4(65) (up minor 6th) instead of A3(57) → F3(53) (down minor 3rd). The subject should be a DESCENDING D minor arpeggio: D4(62)-A3(57)-F3(53)-D3(50), then stepwise motion in the low octave.

Fixed pitches: 62, 57, 53, 50, 49, 50, 52, 53, 55, 53, 52

**Final user message:**
User shared a score screenshot and said: "読めますかね。音価も音高も全部違います。" (Can you read this? Both the note values and pitches are completely different.)

Looking at the score: the first voice shows quarter notes and eighth notes where there should be half notes, and the pitches don't match the Art of Fugue subject. This suggests the exposition's subbeat grid construction is NOT using NoteEvent durations for the subject voice - it's likely treating every beat as a quarter note and running it through the elaborator.

The issue is that I was about to investigate `Phase F: サブビートグリッド構築` in realize_exposition to see how the subject voice's grid is built. I found the relevant code location (line 1672) but hadn't read or fixed it yet when the summary was requested.

There are likely two main problems:
1. The exposition grid construction treats all beats equally (doesn't use NoteEvent durations for the subject voice)
2. `fit_melody_to_range()` transposes subject pitches that fall outside the entry voice's range (D3-D4 spans a wide range that may not fit in any single voice)

Let me also note the key files and their locations.

**GitHub repo**: `https://github.com/nobuhiko-ohki/fuge` (private)
**Working directory**: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/`
**Repo mirror**: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user is building a **Bach-style fugue generator** based on Prout "Fugue" (1891) with ML integration. **GitHub repo**: `https://github.com/nobuhiko-ohki/fuge` (private). Working directory: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/`, repo mirror: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`.

   This session's requests in chronological order:
   1. Continue from previous session — implement C5 removal ("C5は一旦止めてみましょう") and C3 strengthening (root and third individually required, not just simultaneous absence)
   2. Generate fugue with "Die Kunst der Fuge" BWV 1080 Contrapunctus I basic subject: "テーマを「フーガの技法」の基本主題にして生成できますか?"
   3. Fix the rhythm: "リズムが違いますね。冒頭から、二分音符五つ、四分音符二つ、付点二分音符一つ、八分音符三つです。" — The subject must use proper note durations (NoteEvents), not uniform quarter notes. Final D is NOT part of subject ("含めない").
   4. Fix the pitches: "今度は主題が全然違ってますよ!" — Subject should be descending D minor arpeggio (D4→A3→F3→D3), not D4→A3→F4→D4.
   5. Latest: User shared score screenshot showing the output is STILL wrong: "読めますかね。音価も音高も全部違います。" — Both pitches and note durations are completely wrong in the rendered output despite the source data being corrected.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **NoteEvent**: Dataclass with `pitch: Pitch` and `duration: int` (subbeat units: 16th=1, 8th=2, quarter=4, half=8, dotted half=12)
   - **Subject**: Accepts either Pitch list (all quarter notes, backward compat) or NoteEvent list (varying durations). `get_length()` returns beat count (ceiling division), `get_length_subbeats()` returns total subbeats.
   - **`_extract_beat_head_pcs()`**: Extracts pitch class at each beat boundary for harmonic analysis. Must handle notes spanning multiple beats (half notes cover 2 beats, etc.)
   - **`_verify_and_repair_chord_coverage()`**: Post-DP verification ensuring root+third individual presence. 3-stage: (1) substitute chords (2) voice modification (3) chord reassignment + voice modification combo
   - **`_build_subbeat_grid()` / Phase F**: Converts beat-level melodies to subbeat-level grid with rhythm elaboration. **Currently the suspected source of the bug** — may not properly use NoteEvent durations for subject voice in exposition.
   - **`fit_melody_to_range()`**: Transposes pitches to fit within a voice's range. May be distorting the subject when its range (D3-D4) doesn't fit the entry voice.
   - **VOICE_RANGES**: soprano ~[60,84], alto ~[53,74], tenor ~[48,67], bass ~[40,60]
   - **CONSTRAINTS.md**: Design constraint document with [理論] (theory) vs [工学] (engineering) distinction. C5 is currently suspended.
   - **test_constraints.py**: 9 automated regression tests. "Sounding at beat head" methodology (not just "starting at beat head").

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py`** — Main realization engine (most heavily modified)

     **`_extract_beat_head_pcs()` (fixed)** — Was only capturing notes starting ON beat boundaries. Fixed to capture all beat boundaries within each note's span:
     ```python
     @staticmethod
     def _extract_beat_head_pcs(subject: Subject) -> List[int]:
         beat_pcs = []
         subbeat_pos = 0
         next_beat_boundary = 0
         for note in subject.notes:
             note_end = subbeat_pos + note.duration
             while next_beat_boundary < note_end:
                 beat_pcs.append(note.pitch.pitch_class)
                 next_beat_boundary += 4
             subbeat_pos = note_end
         return beat_pcs
     ```

     **`_check_hard()` (fixed)** — Added None check for fixed voices:
     ```python
     prev_fixed = melody[beat - 1]
     curr_fixed = melody[beat]
     # 固定声部が休符(None)の拍はスキップ
     if curr_fixed is None or prev_fixed is None:
         continue
     ```

     **`_score_transition()` (fixed)** — Added None checks in two places:
     - In the motion type scoring loop (line ~901)
     - In the chromatic clash detection loop (line ~948)

     **`_verify_and_repair_chord_coverage()` enhanced** — Now accepts `diatonic_chords` parameter. Enhanced with:
     - Local `_get_dia()` helper using passed diatonic chords
     - Duplicate PC detection in step (2): allows modifying voices that provide root/third if the same PC is covered by another voice
     - Step (3a): Pure chord reassignment from all 7 diatonic chords
     - Step (3b): Combined chord reassignment + 1 voice modification
     
     Each caller now passes local key's diatonic chords:
     - Episode: `_ep_dia_analyzer.diatonic_chords` (from end key)
     - Middle entry: `analyzer.diatonic_chords` (from target key)
     - Coda: `_coda_analyzer.diatonic_chords` (from self.key)

     **Phase F (line 1672)** — Exposition subbeat grid construction. This is the **suspected source of the current bug** — likely not using NoteEvent durations for the subject voice, and `fit_melody_to_range()` may be distorting pitches. **NOT YET EXAMINED/FIXED.**

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_structure.py`** — Subject class

     **`Subject.get_length()` (fixed)** — Changed from floor to ceiling division:
     ```python
     def get_length(self) -> int:
         """主題の長さ(拍数 = 四分音符換算、天井除算)"""
         sb = self.get_length_subbeats()
         return (sb + 3) // 4
     ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/CONSTRAINTS.md`** — Design constraints
     - C5 marked as suspended (一時停止) as of 2026-03-06
     - C3 strengthened: root and third individually required

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/test_constraints.py`** — Regression tests
     - C3 test strengthened: checks individual root/third presence (not just simultaneous absence), with exceptions for final 2 beats (cadence)
     - C3 and C11 tests: Changed note collection from "starts at beat head" to "sounding at beat head":
     ```python
     for beat in range(first_beat, last_beat + 1):
         beat_tick = beat * ticks_per_beat
         if start_tick <= beat_tick < end_tick:
             # register note as sounding at this beat
     ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_art_of_fugue.py`** — Art of Fugue generation script
     - Current subject definition (pitches corrected, rhythm specified):
     ```python
     ART_OF_FUGUE_NOTES = [
         NoteEvent(Pitch(62), 8),   # D4  二分音符  ─┐
         NoteEvent(Pitch(57), 8),   # A3  二分音符   │ 下行分散和音
         NoteEvent(Pitch(53), 8),   # F3  二分音符   │ (Dm: D-A-F-D)
         NoteEvent(Pitch(50), 8),   # D3  二分音符  ─┘
         NoteEvent(Pitch(49), 8),   # C#3 二分音符  ← 導音
         NoteEvent(Pitch(50), 4),   # D3  四分音符  ─┐
         NoteEvent(Pitch(52), 4),   # E3  四分音符   │ 順次上行
         NoteEvent(Pitch(53), 12),  # F3  付点二分音符│
         NoteEvent(Pitch(55), 2),   # G3  八分音符   │
         NoteEvent(Pitch(53), 2),   # F3  八分音符  ─┘ 回帰
         NoteEvent(Pitch(52), 2),   # E3  八分音符
     ]
     ```
     - 3 voices, D minor, tempo=60, seed=42

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_long_no_passing.py`** — Original C major generation script (unchanged, still works)

4. Errors and Fixes:

   - **C3 test failures (10 violations)**: After strengthening C3 to check individual root/third presence
     - Fix 1: Added step (3) chord reassignment fallback — reduced to 6 violations
     - Fix 2: Added `diatonic_chords` parameter to repair function so episodes/middle entries use local key's chords — some improvement
     - Fix 3: Added duplicate PC detection — allows modifying voice that provides root/third when another voice provides the same PC
     - Fix 4: **Critical** — Changed test methodology from "note starts at beat head" to "note sounding at beat head". The test was missing notes that started as 8th-note elaboration in the previous beat but sustained through the current beat head. This was the ROOT CAUSE of remaining test failures.
     - Result: All 9 tests PASS

   - **`_extract_beat_head_pcs()` bug causing infinite hang**: With NoteEvent-based subject (66 subbeats, 17 beats), the old code only captured notes that START on beat boundaries. A half note (8 subbeats) covering 2 beats only registered for the first beat. Result: only 10 beat_pcs generated instead of 17, causing downstream analysis to hang.
     - Fix: Changed while condition from `next_beat_boundary <= subbeat_pos and next_beat_boundary < subbeat_pos + note.duration` to `next_beat_boundary < note_end`

   - **DP TypeError: NoneType in `_check_hard()`**: Fixed voices could have None entries when a voice hasn't entered yet or is resting
     - Fix: Added `if curr_fixed is None or prev_fixed is None: continue`

   - **DP TypeError: NoneType in `_score_transition()`**: Same None issue in two places — motion scoring and chromatic clash detection
     - Fix: Added None checks before arithmetic operations on fixed voice pitches

   - **Wrong pitches for Art of Fugue subject**: User: "今度は主題が全然違ってますよ!" Had F4(65) instead of F3(53), D4(62) instead of D3(50), etc. — the subject should be a DESCENDING arpeggio, not ascending then descending.
     - Fix: Corrected MIDI values from [62,57,65,62,61,62,64,65,67,65,64] to [62,57,53,50,49,50,52,53,55,53,52]

   - **CURRENT UNFIXED BUG**: User shared score showing both pitches and rhythms are STILL wrong in output: "読めますかね。音価も音高も全部違います。" 
     - Suspected causes: (1) Exposition's Phase F subbeat grid construction doesn't use NoteEvent durations for subject voice — treats every beat as a quarter note and elaborates. (2) `fit_melody_to_range()` transposes subject pitches that fall outside the entry voice's range (D3=50 is below soprano range [60,84]).

5. Problem Solving:
   - **SOLVED**: C5 removal and C3 strengthening with full regression test pass
   - **SOLVED**: NoteEvent-based subject with varying durations — `_extract_beat_head_pcs()`, `get_length()` ceiling division, DP None checks
   - **SOLVED**: Correct pitches for Art of Fugue descending arpeggio
   - **IN PROGRESS**: Output MIDI doesn't match specified subject — pitches and rhythms are wrong in the rendered score. Need to investigate exposition's Phase F (subbeat grid construction, line 1672) and `fit_melody_to_range()` behavior with the wide-range subject (D3-D4).

### queue-operation

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Analysis:
Let me chronologically analyze this conversation, which continues from two previous compacted sessions about a Bach-style fugue generator.

**Previous context (from compaction summary):**
- Building a fugue generator based on Prout "Fugue" (1891) with ML integration
- GitHub repo: `https://github.com/nobuhiko-ohki/fuge` (private)
- Working directory: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/`, repo mirror: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`
- BWV 1080 (Art of Fugue) subject was being implemented
- Multiple bugs had been fixed: beat expansion, subject_beats, fit_melody_to_range, first note octave, rhythm correction
- Accidental analysis was in progress
- Modulation structure had been extracted but not yet presented

**This session's conversation flow:**

1. I presented the modulation structure (continuing from previous session)
2. User corrected my error about "A7はト短調の属七" - A7 is NOT G minor's V7, it's D minor's V7
3. User questioned why Episode 1 goes to G minor if Middle Entry 1 is in F major - I found my error was mixing up episode_key_path data between episodes
4. User asked about m7.2-7.3 Ab(=G#) in E7 appearing in the exposition which should be D minor
5. I explained it as V7/V (Doppeldominant/secondary dominant) but E7→F resolution was found to be problematic
6. User questioned if Doppeldominant is appropriate for fugues - I clarified it's not the chord itself but the lack of resolution
7. User asked about the cause of E7→F progression - traced to _try_secondary_dominant() placing E7 but _verify_and_repair changing the resolution target
8. User asked why _try_secondary_dominant() is called at all - found it's called randomly (10% chance) on ANY beat, not just before dominant motion
9. User asked if it's only called before dominant motion - confirmed NO, called on all beats
10. User expressed the listening experience: "短調の曲で変な場所で臨時記号付きの7thがやたら出てきて、どこに向かっているのかわからなくなる"
11. User asked to check Prout's textbook for guidance
12. User then asked to list altered chords containing the augmented 4th that are permitted in classical harmony
13. I listed Italian, French, German augmented sixth chords
14. User asked which are usable in minor keys - all three, since ♭VI is natural in minor
15. User asked about Bach's actual practice with augmented 6th chords in fugues - I explained Bach mostly treats G# as part of dominant harmony (V or vii°), not as altered chords
16. User agreed and said the correct approach is to analyze the answer in the dominant key
17. User also asked about expanding to 4 voices

**Implementation phase:**
18. Implemented three changes simultaneously:
    - Answer harmonic analysis using dominant key (A minor) analyzer
    - _select_for_beat fallback changed from secondary dominant to V
    - 4-voice expansion with realize_fugue() restructured

19. Found get_dominant_key() returns A major, not A minor - fixed to use A minor for minor key fugues
20. Also fixed key_me3 (middle entry 3) to use A minor instead of A major

21. Generated 4-voice piece (39 measures), verified secondary dominants reduced from many to just 2

22. User listened and described it as "不思議な音楽" (strange music), compared to WTC Book 1 No. 24

23. I gave honest assessment: voice range violations, semitone clashes (20+), augmented intervals

24. User asked if voice range fixes would be easy - I incorrectly said the subject spans "完全11度" then corrected to "完全4度"

25. User corrected the subject range as "主音から見て完全5度上から短2度下" (perfect 5th above to minor 2nd below tonic = minor 7th total)

26. User then shared that Bach's Contrapunctus I handles G# as G#dim7 (vii°7), interpretable as E7 substitute

27. User asked about the main cause of semitone clashes and augmented intervals - I explained it's the DP not checking for semitone clashes between voices

28. User corrected: C# locations should ALWAYS be V (A or A7) because it's the leading tone. The subject's implicit harmony should be respected.

29. User asked about the harmonic plan collision - I explained the current system builds entry-specific plans independently

30. User identified the fundamental architectural problem: the system should be top-down (全体構成→転調計画→和声進行→代理和音) not bottom-up

31. User said "最初からそうなっているはずでした" and compared current approach to "コルトレーンクアルテットでバッハ風のフーガを即興しようとするようなもの"

32. Entered plan mode to design top-down harmonic planning

33. Launched explore and plan agents

34. Asked user about how to define subject's implicit harmony - user chose "両方" (both manual specification and improved analyzer)

**Key files modified this session:**
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py` - Multiple changes
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_art_of_fugue.py` - num_voices=4

**Current state:** In plan mode, designing top-down harmonic planning system. Plan file at `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/.claude/plans/imperative-cuddling-feather.md`. User has answered the clarifying question (chose "両方" - both manual and algorithmic). Need to write final plan and call ExitPlanMode.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user is building a **Bach-style fugue generator** based on Prout "Fugue" (1891) with ML integration. **GitHub repo**: `https://github.com/nobuhiko-ohki/fuge` (private). Working directory: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/`, repo mirror: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`.

   This session's requests in chronological order:
   1. Continue from previous session: present the modulation structure of the generated piece
   2. Investigate why E7 (secondary dominant) appears in the exposition and causes E7→F (invalid resolution)
   3. Trace the root cause of secondary dominant insertion (random 10%, no harmonic context)
   4. Discuss augmented sixth chords containing augmented 4th (Italian, French, German +6)
   5. Discuss Bach's actual practice: G# handled as part of V or vii° in dominant key, not as altered chords
   6. **Fix answer harmonic analysis**: use dominant key (A minor) analyzer instead of main key (D minor) analyzer
   7. **Fix _select_for_beat fallback**: replace secondary dominant fallback with V (dominant)
   8. **Expand to 4 voices**: change num_voices from 3 to 4, extend realize_fugue() structure
   9. After listening to the result: evaluate quality honestly
   10. **Current major task**: Redesign the exposition's harmonic planning from bottom-up (per-entry independent plans) to **top-down** (single authoritative plan derived from subject's implicit harmony, all voices follow it)
   11. User chose "両方" (both) for defining subject harmony: manual specification takes priority, algorithmic derivation as fallback

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **NoteEvent**: Dataclass with `pitch: Pitch` and `duration: int` (subbeat units: 16th=1, 8th=2, quarter=4, half=8, half+8th tie=10)
   - **Subject's implicit harmonic progression**: The subject inherently implies a harmonic framework (e.g., C# = leading tone → V is inviolable). This should be the AUTHORITATIVE source for all harmony in the exposition.
   - **Top-down vs bottom-up harmony**: Current system builds per-entry chord plans independently and picks "first entry wins" at overlaps. Correct approach: 全体構成→転調計画→和声進行→代理和音 (overall structure → modulation plan → harmonic progression → substitute chords)
   - **Secondary dominant problem**: `_try_secondary_dominant()` was called randomly (10% chance) on ANY beat regardless of harmonic context, producing E7→F and similar invalid progressions
   - **`_select_for_beat` fallback**: When a pitch class wasn't found in diatonic chords, the code unconditionally returned a secondary dominant chord, bypassing the `secondary_dom_freq` probability guard entirely
   - **Dominant key analysis for answer**: Answer in D minor fugue should be analyzed with A minor (属短調) analyzer, not D minor, so G# is simply V's third (E-G#-B), not a "non-diatonic" note requiring secondary dominant
   - **Augmented sixth chords**: Italian (B♭-D-G#), French (B♭-D-E-G#), German (B♭-D-F-G#) - all contain #IV, resolve to V. All usable in minor. But Bach rarely uses them in fugue expositions.
   - **Bach's practice for G# in minor fugues**: Treats it as part of V (A major) or vii° (G#dim), NOT as altered chords or secondary dominants
   - **I-II-V-I framework**: User emphasized that classical harmony operates within this fundamental progression; secondary dominants only appear within this framework, not randomly
   - **_verify_and_repair_chord_coverage**: Post-hoc repair that can change both chords AND voice pitches. In the new design, it should NEVER change the chord plan.
   - **VOICE_RANGES**: soprano (60,79), alto (55,74), tenor (48,67), bass (40,60) - Piston-based, but for keyboard fugues these are not strict constraints
   - **BWV 1080 subject**: D3(50)-A3(57)-F3(53)-D3(50)-C#3(49)-D3(50)-E3(52)-F3(53)-G3(55)-F3(53)-E3(52), 64 subbeats = 16 beats, range: C#3 to A3 (minor 7th)
   - **Modulation structure** (corrected): Dm → F major (平行調) → G minor (下属調) → A minor (属短調) → Dm
   - **4-voice exposition order**: Alto→Soprano→Bass→Tenor (Prout Ch.I §5)

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py`** — Main realization engine (most heavily modified)

     **Change 1: Answer harmonic analysis switched to dominant key** (line ~1536-1551):
     ```python
     # 応答は属調のアナライザで分析
     # 属短調(例: D minor → A minor)のダイアトニック和音で分析することで
     # G# 等の属調固有音が副属七和音に逃げず、自然なV→Iに収まる
     # 短調の属調は属短調(和声的短音階)を使用
     dom_pc = self.key.dominant_pc
     from fugue_structure import PC_TO_NOTE
     dom_note = PC_TO_NOTE.get(dom_pc, 'A')
     dom_key = Key(dom_note, "minor" if self.key.mode == "minor" else "major")
     dom_analyzer = SubjectHarmonicAnalyzer(
         dom_key, seed=self.seed,
         seventh_freq=0.0,
         altered_freq=0.0,
         secondary_dom_freq=0.0,
     )
     answer_chord_plan = dom_analyzer.analyze(answer)
     ```

     **Change 2: `_select_for_beat` fallback** (line ~609-615):
     ```python
     candidates = self.find_containing_chords(pitch_class)
     if not candidates:
         # 音階外音 → V(属和音)にフォールバック
         # 古典和声の原則: 音階外音は多くの場合ドミナント領域で生じる
         # 副属七和音への安易なフォールバックは調性を曖昧にするため禁止
         return self.diatonic_chords[4]  # V(属和音)
     ```

     **Change 3: `realize_fugue()` restructured for 4-voice support** (line ~2858-2997):
     - Added helper functions `_do_episode()` and `_do_middle_entry()` to reduce code duplication
     - 4-voice structure: Expo→Ep1→ME1(平行調)→Ep2→ME2(下属調)→Ep3→ME3(属調)→Coda
     - 3-voice structure preserved as fallback
     - `key_me3` uses A minor (not A major from `get_dominant_key()`) for minor key fugues:
     ```python
     # 4声の場合: 中間部3 = 属調(短調では属短調を使用)
     dom_key_raw = mod_plan[1][1] if len(mod_plan) > 1 else self.key
     if self.key.mode == "minor" and dom_key_raw.mode == "major":
         from fugue_structure import PC_TO_NOTE
         key_me3 = Key(PC_TO_NOTE.get(dom_key_raw.tonic_pc, 'A'), "minor")
     else:
         key_me3 = dom_key_raw
     ```

     **Critical existing code - Phase C exposition_chords construction** (lines 1595-1611, TO BE REDESIGNED):
     ```python
     for beat in range(total_beats):
         chord = None
         for entry in entries:
             rel = beat - entry.start_position
             if 0 <= rel < subject_len:
                 plan = (answer_chord_plan if entry.is_answer
                         else self.chord_plan)
                 if rel < len(plan):
                     chord = plan[rel]
                 break  # ← FIRST MATCH WINS - THIS IS THE ROOT PROBLEM
         if chord is None:
             chord = self.analyzer.diatonic_chords[0]  # I
         self.exposition_chords.append(chord)
     ```

     **`_verify_and_repair_chord_coverage()`** (lines 3158-3392):
     - Three-tier repair: substitute chord → voice modification → combined chord+voice fix
     - Currently can modify BOTH chords and voices
     - In new design: should only modify voices, NEVER the chord plan

     **`_try_secondary_dominant()`** (lines 493-508):
     ```python
     def _try_secondary_dominant(
         self, pitch_class: int, next_chord: ChordLabel,
     ) -> Optional[ChordLabel]:
         target_degree = next_chord.degree
         if target_degree not in self.secondary_dominants:
             return None
         sec_dom = self.secondary_dominants[target_degree]
         if pitch_class in sec_dom.tones:
             return sec_dom
         return None
     ```
     Called from `_apply_extended_harmony()` (line 466): `if beat + 1 < length and self.rng.random() < self.secondary_dom_freq`
     - Called on ANY beat (not just before dominant), no harmonic context check
     - `secondary_dom_freq=0.10` for episodes, `0.05` for middle entries, `0.0` for exposition

     **`SubjectHarmonicAnalyzer` secondary_dom_freq settings across contexts**:
     - Exposition analyzer (line 1484): `secondary_dom_freq=0.0`
     - Episode analyzers (lines 2148, 2189): `secondary_dom_freq=0.10` — still problematic
     - Middle entry analyzer (line 2429): `secondary_dom_freq=0.05` — still problematic
     - Coda analyzer (line 2794): `secondary_dom_freq=0.0`
     - All transition/key-change analyzers: `secondary_dom_freq=0.0`

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_art_of_fugue.py`** — Art of Fugue generation script

     **Change: num_voices changed from 3 to 4** (line 101):
     ```python
     structure = FugueStructure(num_voices=4, main_key=key, subject=subject)
     ```

     **Subject definition (unchanged from previous session)**:
     ```python
     ART_OF_FUGUE_NOTES = [
         NoteEvent(Pitch(50), 8),   # D3  二分音符  ─ 主音(低オクターブ)
         NoteEvent(Pitch(57), 8),   # A3  二分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(53), 8),   # F3  二分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(50), 8),   # D3  二分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(49), 8),   # C#3 二分音符  ← 導音
         NoteEvent(Pitch(50), 4),   # D3  四分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(52), 4),   # E3  四分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(53), 10),  # F3  二分+八分タイ
         NoteEvent(Pitch(55), 2),   # G3  八分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(53), 2),   # F3  八分音符
         NoteEvent(Pitch(52), 2),   # E3  八分音符
     ]
     ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_structure.py`** — Subject, Key, FugueStructure classes

     **`get_dominant_key()`** (line 128): Returns A **major** for D minor — this is the source of the issue requiring manual override for minor keys
     ```python
     def get_dominant_key(self) -> 'Key':
         dom_pc = self.dominant_pc
         return Key(PC_TO_NOTE.get(dom_pc, 'G'), "major")
     ```

     **`_get_voice_order()`** (line 908): 4-voice order already defined:
     ```python
     else:
         return [
             FugueVoiceType.ALTO,
             FugueVoiceType.SOPRANO,
             FugueVoiceType.BASS,
             FugueVoiceType.TENOR,
         ]
     ```

     **`get_modulation_plan()`** (line 1014): Returns [主調, 属調, 平行調, 下属調, 主調]

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/CONSTRAINTS.md`** — Design constraints document
     - C1: Only V7 and vii°7 seventh chords allowed (engineering constraint)
     - C2: seventh_freq=0.0 everywhere
     - C3: Root and third must be present in 2+ voice beats (theory constraint)
     - C14-C18: Unimplemented constraints (leading tone resolution, doubling prohibition, V7 seventh resolution, augmented interval prohibition, voice crossing prohibition)

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **"A7はト短調の属七" error**: I incorrectly stated A7 is V7 of G minor. A7 is V7 of D minor. G minor's V7 is D7. User corrected immediately.
   - **Episode key path confusion**: I said episode_key_path showed Dm→Gm for Episode 1, but Episode 1's end_key is actually F major (key_me1). I had confused Episode 1 with Episode 2. User caught the inconsistency: "嬉遊部1は中間提示1のヘ長調への橋渡しではないのですか?"
   - **Subject range error**: I said the subject spans "完全11度" (perfect 11th), then corrected to "完全4度" (perfect 4th). User further corrected: the range is C#3 to A3, which is "主音から見て完全5度上から短2度下" — a minor 7th total.
   - **get_dominant_key() returns A major instead of A minor**: For minor key fugues, the dominant key for analysis should be minor (A minor, not A major). A minor's diatonic chords correctly include E major (with G#). Fixed by manually constructing the key.
   - **key_me3 using A major for middle entry 3**: Same issue — fixed with explicit check for minor mode.
   - **_select_for_beat secondary dominant fallback bypassing freq guard**: The `secondary_dom_freq=0.0` setting was ineffective because `_select_for_beat()` had an independent code path (lines 609-623) that unconditionally returned secondary dominants for non-diatonic pitch classes. Fixed by replacing with V (dominant) fallback.

5. Problem Solving:
   - **SOLVED**: E7 (secondary dominant) appearing in exposition — caused by two independent code paths: (1) `_select_for_beat` unconditional secondary dominant fallback for non-diatonic notes, (2) `_apply_extended_harmony` random insertion. Fixed both.
   - **SOLVED**: 4-voice expansion — added 3rd episode and 3rd middle entry (属短調) for 4-voice fugues
   - **SOLVED**: A major vs A minor for dominant key analysis — corrected to use minor for minor key fugues
   - **IN PROGRESS (MAJOR)**: Top-down harmonic planning for exposition. The fundamental architectural problem is that each entry has an independent chord plan, and at overlaps "first entry wins". This causes C vs C# clashes and incoherent harmony. The solution is to build a single authoritative harmonic plan for the entire exposition before generating any counterpoint.
   - **IDENTIFIED but not yet addressed**: 
     - Half-tone clashes (C vs C#, F vs F#, etc.) — 20+ occurrences
     - Augmented melodic intervals (C→A augmented 2nd, C#→G diminished 5th)
     - Parallel 5ths/8ths — 8 errors
     - Voice crossing — many occurrences (lower priority for keyboard music)

### queue-operation

元々は、バッハ風のフーガを自動生成したいのですが、機械学習に全面的に頼って、バッハの音楽技術全体を彼が受け継いだ伝統的な技術を含めて再発見するのは困難だろうから、和声学や対位法、当時の作曲技法、あるいはバッハ固有の既知の技法などを機械学習の骨格として備えるのが狙いだったと思います。
この視点で現状の大まかな達成状況と、課題、そして対策をざっとまとめて、そこから各論に展開していくというステップを取らないと、また迷路を自ら生成して駆けずり回ることになると思います。

### queue-operation

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Analysis:
Let me chronologically analyze this conversation carefully.

**Session Context**: This is a continuation from two previous sessions about a Bach-style fugue generator. The summary from the previous session indicates work on top-down harmonic planning, forbidden_pcs system (which caused problems), and architectural discussions about VNS-based iterative refinement.

**Message 1 (System/Continuation)**: Detailed summary of previous work including forbidden_pcs issues, architectural problems with the three-layer pipeline, and the user's insight about rhythm as a harmonic tool.

**My First Action**: Research computational models for counterpoint generation (VNS, MCMC, MCTS, CSP, etc.) to address user's question "なんかいいモデルはないですかね"

**User Message 1**: "いきましょう" (Let's go) - approving the VNS approach.

**My Actions**: 
1. Rolled back forbidden_pcs from elaborate_beat, _pick_eighth_note, _passing_toward, _neighbor_tone, _build_subbeat_grid
2. Created vns_refiner.py with LexScore (lexicographic ordering), evaluate_beat, 5 neighborhood moves (N1-N5), VNSRefiner class
3. Integrated VNS into realize_exposition() as Phase G
4. Generated test: VNS initial L0=16→final L0=2, errors=46, warnings=51

**User Message 2**: "続けてください" (Continue) - I was in the middle of rollback edits

**User Message 3**: "errors 48→46, warnings 85→51の意味は?"
- I explained that errors/warnings come from FugueQualityChecker covering the entire piece, while VNS only operates on exposition (67 of 159 beats).

**User Message 4**: "だんだん何をやっているかわからなくなっていました。現状、課題、対策を整理し直すことをする必要がありますか?"
- User lost track, wants to reorganize.

**User Message 5**: "もっと大局的な話ができませんか?元々は、バッハ風のフーガを自動生成したいのですが..."
- KEY MESSAGE: User wants a big-picture assessment. The original goal is hybrid ML + music theory for Bach fugue generation. User worried about getting lost in details ("迷路を自ら生成して駆けずり回る").

**My Action**: Created OVERVIEW.md with comprehensive assessment of all Bach fugue techniques needed, implementation status (◎/○/△/✗), identified 3 structural problems:
1. No countersubject
2. No sequences in episodes  
3. Incomplete theory rules

**User Message 6**: "対主題の定義は?"
- I explained countersubject: melody that accompanies subject from 2nd entry onwards, with 3 conditions (harmonic compatibility, rhythmic independence, reusability/invertible counterpoint)

**User Message 7**: "提示部において主題以外のパートに単なる伴奏以外の、再利用、共通化可能な特性を持たせようとしているわけですね。それは主題と同様、一種の旋律的な要素で、主題との関係において、法則化あるいは定量化可能な特性が存在すると仮定して良いのですか?"
- I confirmed: yes, interval rules (3rds/6ths preferred), rhythmic complementarity, invertible counterpoint constraints are all quantifiable.

**User Message 8**: "これは、言い換えれば、既存の和声的要請に加えた、対位法的要請ですよね。これは現状何も含まれていないわけではないが、機能として独立してまとめようとしているわけですか?"
- I clarified: not replacing existing counterpoint constraints (which are local/beat-by-beat), but adding long-range constraints (subject-wide interval profile, rhythmic complementarity, invertibility). It layers on top of existing DP.

**User Message 9**: "これはおそらく対旋律に対してある種、独立した個性を与えることになりそうですね。私は過剰な制約を加えることを心配しているのですが、まあやってみましょう。"
- User concerned about over-constraining but agreed to proceed. I committed to keeping constraints SOFT (scoring bonuses, not hard prohibitions).

**My Implementation Actions**:
1. Added `cs_profile` parameter to ContrapuntalDP.generate() - soft bonus for matching target pitches
2. Added countersubject profile scoring in _score_transition() - ±2.0 to -0.3 bonus based on distance
3. Modified realize_exposition() Phase D(b) to:
   - Save first DP result as countersubject (entry_idx==1)
   - For entry_idx>=2, transpose countersubject and pass as cs_profile
4. Expanded DP candidates from chord tones only to all diatonic scale tones (with `_key_scale`)

**Error**: First test showed countersubject as "音域 64-64" (all same note E4). Root cause: DP candidates were chord-tones-only (3 PCs), too restrictive for melodic generation. Fixed by expanding to all diatonic scale tones.

**Second test**: Countersubject "音域 55-57" (G3-A3), only 2-3 notes. Root cause: voice range problem - subject D3 far below Alto range G3, squeezing countersubject into tiny space.

**User Message 10**: "声域逸脱問題がそんなに気になるなら、調を適当に移調してください。"
- User said to just transpose to fix the range issue.

**My Action**: Transposed all subject notes up 1 octave (+12): D3→D4 (50→62), etc.

**Final test result**: 
- Countersubject: ['C4', 'C4', 'A3', 'G3', 'A3', 'A3', 'C4', 'D4', 'E4', 'F4', 'E4', 'D4', 'A3', 'G3', 'A3', 'Ab3'] - much more melodic, range 55-65
- VNS: L0=8→0, L1=24→0, L2=4→0 (perfect convergence at iter 21!)
- errors=7, warnings=64
- Voice range errors should be dramatically reduced

Key files:
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py` - main engine
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/vns_refiner.py` - new VNS module
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_art_of_fugue.py` - generation script
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/OVERVIEW.md` - big picture assessment
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/CONSTRAINTS.md` - design constraints
- Repo mirror: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user is building a **Bach-style fugue generator** with a hybrid ML + music theory approach. The original vision: classical harmony, counterpoint, Baroque composition techniques, and Bach-specific methods form the **skeleton**, while ML (trained on Bach WTC corpus) fills the gaps. **GitHub repo**: `https://github.com/nobuhiko-ohki/fuge` (private). Working directory: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/`, repo mirror: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`.

   This session focused on:
   - Implementing VNS (Variable Neighborhood Search) iterative refinement to replace the failed forbidden_pcs approach
   - Rolling back forbidden_pcs completely
   - Big-picture reassessment of the project (OVERVIEW.md) — identifying that **countersubject generation** is the most impactful next step
   - Implementing countersubject generation and reuse across exposition entries
   - Expanding DP candidates from chord-tones-only to all diatonic scale tones
   - Transposing the subject up 1 octave to fix voice range violations

   The user explicitly emphasized wanting a **big-picture view** rather than getting lost in implementation details. Quote: "また迷路を自ら生成して駆けずり回ることになると思います" (we'll end up generating our own maze and running around in it).

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **VNS (Variable Neighborhood Search)**: Metaheuristic local search with 5 neighborhood types (pitch change, rhythm pattern, note extension, displacement, passing tone swap)
   - **Lexicographic ordering (LexScore)**: Non-additive scoring with 4 levels: L0(fatal: parallel 5ths/8ves, voice crossing) > L1(harmony: semitone clashes, chord coverage) > L2(melody: leaps, trill patterns) > L3(aesthetic)
   - **Countersubject (対主題)**: Recurring counter-melody accompanying the subject, with 3 requirements: harmonic compatibility (3rds/6ths preferred), rhythmic complementarity, reusability via transposition
   - **cs_profile**: Soft guidance for DP — transposed countersubject target pitches, with distance-based bonus (not hard constraint)
   - **Diatonic scale candidate expansion**: DP candidates expanded from chord tones only (~3 PCs) to all diatonic scale tones (~7 PCs), enabling stepwise melodic motion
   - **Invertible counterpoint at the octave**: When voices swap, 3rds↔6ths (good), but 5ths→4ths (bad). Avoid 5ths in countersubject.
   - **Subject harmonic template (SubjectHarmonicTemplate)**: Per-beat harmony specs with fixed_pcs and flexibility levels
   - **BeatHarmony**: degree, quality, fixed_pcs, flexibility per beat
   - **NoteEvent**: `pitch: Pitch`, `duration: int` (subbeat units: 16th=1, 8th=2, quarter=4, half=8)
   - **BWV 1080 subject (now octave-shifted)**: D4(62)-A4(69)-F4(65)-D4(62)-C#4(61)-D4(62)-E4(64)-F4(65)-G4(67)-F4(65)-E4(64), 64 subbeats = 16 beats

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/vns_refiner.py`** — NEW file, ~500 lines
     - Core VNS refinement module operating on subbeat grids
     - LexScore dataclass with lexicographic comparison
     - evaluate_beat() checks: voice crossing, parallel 5ths/8ves, semitone clashes, chord coverage, melodic leaps, trill patterns
     - 5 neighborhood move classes: PitchChangeMove(N1), RhythmPatternMove(N2), NoteExtensionMove(N3), DisplacementMove(N4), PassingToneSwapMove(N5)
     - VNSRefiner.refine() main loop: identify worst beats → generate moves → apply best improving move → iterate
     - Key design: problem-driven (targets worst beats, not random), candidate sampling (max 30 per iteration), patience-based termination

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py`** — Main engine (~3750 lines), heavily modified

     **forbidden_pcs complete removal**: Removed `forbidden_pcs` parameter from:
     - `elaborate_beat()` (line ~1286)
     - `_pick_eighth_note()` (line ~1355)
     - `_passing_toward()` (line ~1443)
     - `_neighbor_tone()` (line ~1469)
     - `_build_subbeat_grid()` signature and forbidden calculation block (line ~3267)
     - Calling site in realize_exposition() (line ~1929)

     **DP candidate expansion** (line ~783):
     ```python
     scale_pcs = set(chord_plan[0].tones)  # fallback
     if hasattr(self, '_key_scale'):
         scale_pcs = self._key_scale
     candidates_per_beat = []
     for beat in range(num_beats):
         chord_tones_pc = chord_plan[beat].tones
         cands = []
         for midi in range(lo, hi + 1):
             pc = midi % 12
             if pc in chord_tones_pc or pc in scale_pcs:
                 cands.append(midi)
         ...
     ```

     **cs_profile parameter** added to ContrapuntalDP.generate() (line ~748):
     ```python
     def generate(self, num_beats, chord_plan, voice_range, fixed_voices,
                  free_voice_name, start_from=None, prev_fixed_pitches=None,
                  cs_profile=None) -> List[int]:
     ```

     **Countersubject scoring** added to _score_transition() (after line ~1043):
     ```python
     if hasattr(self, '_cs_profile') and self._cs_profile is not None:
         if beat < len(self._cs_profile) and self._cs_profile[beat] is not None:
             target = self._cs_profile[beat]
             dist = abs(curr_free - target)
             if dist == 0:
                 cost -= 2.0   # exact match bonus
             elif dist <= 2:
                 cost -= 1.0   # within 2 semitones
             elif dist <= 4:
                 cost -= 0.3   # within 4 semitones
     ```

     **Countersubject generation and reuse** in realize_exposition() Phase D(b) (line ~1868):
     - entry_idx==1: Generate countersubject via normal DP, save as `self.countersubject_midi`
     - entry_idx>=2: Transpose saved countersubject to target voice range with octave_shift + interval_shift (subject↔answer), pass as `cs_profile` to DP
     - Key: `interval_shift = 7 if entry.is_answer else -7` when entry type differs from 2nd entry

     **VNS integration** as Phase G (after Phase F, line ~1929):
     ```python
     from vns_refiner import VNSRefiner
     refiner = VNSRefiner(subbeat_grid, exposition_chords, self.key,
                          _subject_beats, total_beats, seed=self.seed, elaborate=self.elaborate)
     subbeat_grid, vns_log = refiner.refine(max_iterations=500, patience=50, verbose=True)
     ```

     **_key_scale injection** (before Phase D):
     ```python
     self.dp._key_scale = set(self.key.scale)
     ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_art_of_fugue.py`** — Generation script
     - Subject notes transposed +12 (octave up): D3(50)→D4(62), A3(57)→A4(69), etc.
     - Added countersubject dump output
     - Harmony template unchanged (fixed_pcs use pitch classes, not absolute MIDI, so octave-independent)

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/OVERVIEW.md`** — NEW file, big-picture assessment
     - Lists all Bach fugue technique requirements with implementation status (◎/○/△/✗)
     - Identifies 3 structural problems: no countersubject, no sequences in episodes, incomplete theory rules
     - Prioritized action plan: short-term (range fix, VNS expansion), mid-term (countersubject, sequences), long-term (invertible counterpoint, augmentation/diminution)

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/CONSTRAINTS.md`** — Design constraints document
     - 18 constraints (C1-C18), classified as [理論] (theory, immutable) or [工学] (engineering, can relax)
     - C14 (leading tone resolution), C15 (no LT doubling), C16 (V7 7th resolution), C17 (augmented intervals), C18 (voice crossing) still unimplemented

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **Countersubject all-same-pitch (64-64)**: First test after cs_profile implementation showed countersubject as all E4. Root cause: DP candidates were chord-tones-only (~3 PCs per beat), leaving almost no melodic choices. Fix: expanded candidates to all diatonic scale tones via `_key_scale`.
   - **Countersubject too narrow (55-57)**: After diatonic expansion, countersubject only used G3-A3. Root cause: BWV 1080 subject (D3) placed in Alto below its range (G3-D5), squeezing the countersubject into 2-3 notes. User's fix directive: "声域逸脱問題がそんなに気になるなら、調を適当に移調してください" → transposed subject up 1 octave.
   - **VNS initial score higher after countersubject (L0=23 vs 16)**: The countersubject profile created slightly different voice leading that increased initial conflicts, but VNS still converged to L0=2.
   - **Import error**: `ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'harmony_rules_complete'` when running from wrong directory. Fix: run from `src/` directory or use the generate script which sets sys.path.
   - **User feedback on approach**: User repeatedly pushed back on getting lost in details:
     - "だんだん何をやっているかわからなくなっていきました" (losing track)
     - "もっと大局的な話ができませんか?" (can we talk big picture?)
     - "また迷路を自ら生成して駆けずり回ることになると思います" (we'll generate our own maze)
     - "私は過剰な制約を加えることを心配しているのですが" (worried about over-constraining)
   - **Previous session errors (context)**: forbidden_pcs caused trill-like artifacts ("八分音符のトリルのようなフーガにしては奇妙な音型"), leading to complete rollback this session.

5. Problem Solving:
   - **SOLVED**: forbidden_pcs trill artifacts → complete rollback, replaced by VNS
   - **SOLVED**: VNS implementation for exposition → L0=16→0 (after octave fix), L1=24→0, L2=4→0
   - **SOLVED**: Countersubject generation and reuse mechanism → cs_profile soft guidance
   - **SOLVED**: DP candidate starvation → expanded from chord tones to diatonic scale tones
   - **SOLVED**: Voice range violations (37 errors) → subject transposed up 1 octave, errors=46→7
   - **PARTIALLY SOLVED**: Countersubject quality → now spans 55-65 (10 semitones) with melodic motion, but quality needs evaluation by listening
   - **NOT YET ADDRESSED**: VNS for post-exposition sections (episodes, middle entries)
   - **NOT YET ADDRESSED**: Sequence generation for episodes
   - **NOT YET ADDRESSED**: C14-C18 constraint implementation
   - **NOT YET ADDRESSED**: Augmented interval avoidance in generation

6. All user messages:
   - "いきましょう。" (Let's go — approving VNS approach)
   - "続けてください。" (Continue — I was mid-rollback)
   - "errors 48→46, warnings 85→51の意味は?" (What do these numbers mean?)
   - "だんだん何をやっているかわからなくなっていきました。現状、課題、対策を整理し直すことをする必要がありますか?" (I'm losing track. Do we need to reorganize current state, issues, and countermeasures?)
   - "もっと大局的な話ができませんか?元々は、バッハ風のフーガを自動生成したいのですが、機械学習に全面的に頼って、バッハの音楽技術全体を彼が受け継いだ伝統的な技術を含めて再発見するのは困難だろうから、和声学や対位法、当時の作曲技法、あるいはバッハ固有の既知の技法などを機械学習の骨格として備えるのが狙いだったと思います。この視点で現状の大まかな達成状況と、課題、そして対策をざっとまとめて、そこから各論に展開していくというステップを取らないと、また迷路を自ら生成して駆けずり回ることになると思います。" (Can we talk big picture? The original goal was hybrid ML + theory. We need overview → issues → strategy → details, or we'll create our own maze.)
   - "対主題の定義は?" (What is the definition of countersubject?)
   - "提示部において主題以外のパートに単なる伴奏以外の、再利用、共通化可能な特性を持たせようとしているわけですね。それは主題と同様、一種の旋律的な要素で、主題との関係において、法則化あるいは定量化可能な特性が存在すると仮定して良いのですか?" (So you're trying to give non-subject voices reusable characteristics. Can we assume the relationship between subject and countersubject has quantifiable rules?)
   - "これは、言い換えれば、既存の和声的要請に加えた、対位法的要請ですよね。これは現状何も含まれていないわけではないが、機能として独立してまとめようとしているわけですか?" (This is contrapuntal requirements added to existing harmonic ones. These aren't absent now, but you're trying to consolidate them as an independent function?)
   - "これはおそらく対旋律に対してある種、独立した個性を与えることになりそうですね。私は過剰な制約を加えることを心配しているのですが、まあやってみましょう。" (This will give countermelody its own personality. I'm worried about over-constraining, but let's try.)
   - "声域逸脱問題がそんなに気になるなら、調を適当に移調してください。" (If the voice range issue bothers you that much, just transpose to an appropriate key.)

7. Pending Tasks:

**User Message 1:** "フォールバックをする仕組みがありながら、なぜこれだけ不協和音の嵐なのでしょう。出力が得られませんでしたというのならわかりますが。"
- Key feedback: User questions why there are still so many dissonances despite having fallback mechanisms (VNS). The system should either fix them or report failure, not silently produce bad output.

**My Investigation:**
1. Found VNS evaluate_beat doesn't check augmented intervals at all (only L0: parallel 5ths/8ves, voice crossing; L1: semitone clashes; L2: leaps, trills)
2. Added augmented interval check to VNS evaluate_beat (L2)
3. Test: warnings 58→41

**User Message 2:** "増音程イコール不協和音ではないですよ。不協和音というより、突然の他調のコードのように聞こえるから駄目なんでしょう。トライトーンは、属七にも、長音階にも含まれていますからね。避けられませんが、C#はフーガの5度上の主題で不可避だからといって無神経に鳴らせばいいわけではない。半音衝突も経過音ならまだしも、隣同士の短二度の衝突はMajor7thを展開系で使わない限りあり得ないし、経過音でも避けるべきでしょう。長二度ですら耳障りですから。"
- Key feedback: 
  - Augmented intervals ≠ dissonance; they sound like sudden foreign keys
  - Tritones exist in dominant 7ths and major scales, unavoidable
  - C# in fugue answer is unavoidable but shouldn't be carelessly placed
  - Semitone clashes (minor 2nds) should be avoided even as passing tones
  - Even major 2nds are harsh

**My Deep Investigation:**
1. Analyzed WHERE problems originate - DP output (before decoration) already has:
   - 4 semitone clashes
   - 15 augmented intervals
2. Root cause in DP: `_score_vertical` only penalizes minor 2nd with cost +3.0, while chord completion bonus is -4.0 (outweighs it!)
3. No augmented interval penalty in `_score_transition` at all

**My Fixes:**
1. `_score_vertical`: minor 2nd penalty 3.0→15.0, separated major 2nd (5.0) from minor 2nd
2. `_score_transition`: Added augmented interval penalties (tritone +20.0, aug2 +15.0)
3. `_score_transition`: Added direct semitone clash penalty (+12.0) for simultaneous sounding with fixed voices
4. Result: DP semitone clashes 4→0, DP augmented intervals 15→13

5. VNS: Moved semitone clash from L1 to L0 (fatal level)
6. VNS: Moved augmented intervals from L2 to L1

7. Checker false positive fix: `_check_chromatic_clash` was aggregating all pitches within a beat across subbeats of the SAME voice. When alto plays C→C# within one beat (decoration), checker reported C vs C# as a clash, but they never sound simultaneously. Fixed to only check inter-voice clashes.

8. Result after all fixes: errors=6, warnings=36 (from initial errors=7, warnings=64)

**Remaining issues:**
- errors=6: parallel 5ths/8ves in episodes/middle entries that VNS can't resolve
- warnings=15 semitone clashes: mostly in modulating sections
- warnings=21 augmented intervals: many from subject itself (C#→G tritone)

**User Message 3:** "Bb-C#の問題はGm->Aの進行を同じ展開型で並べると起きる現象ですよね。展開型を変えて回避するのが普通では?"
- Key feedback: The Bb→C# augmented 2nd happens when you keep the same inversion (voicing) across Gm→A progression. Changing the voicing is the normal way to avoid it.

**My Response:**
- Agreed. The root problem is voicing/voice leading, not penalty tuning
- DP selects individual pitches without systematic voice leading rules
- Need proper voice leading rules (common tone retention, nearest motion, leading tone resolution)

**User Message 4 (most recent):** "私のポイントは、増音程を単純に禁止して仕舞えば、それ以外の組み合わせが必然的に選ばれるということです。計算速度を上げるためには、真っ先に和声学の推奨方法に従うのが賢明だと思いますが、守るべきはまず禁止事項と命令事項です。"
- Key feedback: 
  - Simply prohibit augmented intervals → other combinations will necessarily be chosen
  - For computation speed, following harmony textbook recommendations is wise
  - But the priority is: **prohibitions and imperatives first**
  - This is followed by the summary request

**Key Discovery - Key.scale bug:**
- `Key(2, 'minor').scale` returns `[0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 8, 11]` (C harmonic minor!) instead of D harmonic minor
- `Key('D', 'minor').scale` returns correctly `[2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 10, 1]`
- `Key(2, 'minor').tonic_pc` returns 0, not 2!
- This means the augmented interval detection in both DP and VNS is using wrong scale when Key is constructed with integer

Key files modified:
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py` - DP scoring fixes, VNS additions to all sections
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/vns_refiner.py` - semitone clash to L0, augmented intervals added
- `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_quality_checker.py` - false positive fix in chromatic clash

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user is building a **Bach-style fugue generator** (hybrid ML + music theory). GitHub repo: `https://github.com/nobuhiko-ohki/fuge`. Working directory: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/`, repo mirror: `/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/fuge/`.

   This session focused on:
   - Expanding VNS to all sections (episodes, middle entries, coda) — completed
   - Diagnosing and fixing why dissonances persist despite VNS fallback
   - Strengthening DP scoring to prohibit semitone clashes and augmented intervals
   - Fixing checker false positives for intra-voice chromatic motion
   
   The user's core philosophy (stated repeatedly):
   - **Prohibitions and imperatives come first** — augmented intervals should be simply prohibited, not softly penalized
   - Voicing/inversion changes are the normal way to avoid Bb→C# augmented 2nds (changing chord inversion rather than keeping same voice on 3rd→3rd)
   - Semitone clashes (minor 2nds) should be avoided even as passing tones
   - "フォールバックをする仕組みがありながら、なぜこれだけ不協和音の嵐なのでしょう" — the system should fix problems or report failure, not silently produce bad output
   - "増音程を単純に禁止して仕舞えば、それ以外の組み合わせが必然的に選ばれる" — simply prohibit augmented intervals; other combinations will necessarily be chosen
   - Speed optimization comes from following textbook harmony rules, but **hard prohibitions first**

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **VNS (Variable Neighborhood Search)**: Now applied to ALL sections (exposition, episodes, middle entries, coda). Exposition: max_iterations=500, patience=50. Others: max_iterations=500, patience=50.
   - **LexScore levels**: L0=fatal (parallel 5ths/8ves, voice crossing, **semitone clashes** [moved from L1]), L1=harmony (chord coverage, **augmented intervals** [moved from L2]), L2=melody (leaps, trills), L3=aesthetic
   - **DP scoring hierarchy**: semitone clash +15.0 (vertical) / +12.0 (transition), augmented 2nd +15.0, tritone +20.0, major 2nd +5.0
   - **Checker false positive**: `_check_chromatic_clash` was aggregating all pitches within a beat for the same voice (e.g., alto C→C# decoration counted as simultaneous C+C#). Fixed to only check inter-voice clashes.
   - **Root cause of augmented intervals**: Not a penalty issue but a **voicing/voice leading** issue. Gm→A with same inversion forces Bb→C# (aug2). Changing inversion (Bb→A or Bb→E) avoids it entirely.
   - **Key.scale bug discovered**: `Key(2, 'minor').tonic_pc` returns 0 (not 2), `Key(2, 'minor').scale` returns C harmonic minor instead of D harmonic minor. `Key('D', 'minor')` works correctly. This affects augmented interval detection in DP's `_score_transition` where `self._key_scale` is set from `self.key.scale`.
   - **BWV 1080 subject** (octave-shifted): D4(62)-A4(69)-F4(65)-D4(62)-C#4(61)-D4(62)-E4(64)-F4(65)-G4(67)-F4(65)-E4(64), 64 subbeats = 16 beats

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_realization.py`** (~3800 lines) — Main engine
     - **VNS added to episodes** (after grid construction, before MIDI output ~line 2632):

       from vns_refiner import VNSRefiner
       ep_vns_key = key_path.key_at(0) if key_path else start_key
       ep_refiner = VNSRefiner(
           grid, ep_chord_plan, ep_vns_key,
           _ep_subject_beats, ep_length,
           seed=self.seed, elaborate=self.elaborate)
       grid, _ep_vns_log = ep_refiner.refine(
           max_iterations=500, patience=50, verbose=False)
       ```
     - **VNS added to middle entries** (~line 2840):

           max_iterations=500, patience=50, verbose=False)
       ```
     - **`_score_vertical` fix** — minor 2nd penalty raised from 3.0 to 15.0, separated from major 2nd:
       ```python
       elif ic in {1, 11}:
           cost += 15.0  # 短2度・長7度: 禁止的ペナルティ(半音衝突)
       elif ic in {2, 10}:
           cost += 5.0   # 長2度・短7度: 大ペナルティ
       ```
     - **`_score_transition` augmented interval penalty added**:
       ```python
       # --- 増音程ペナルティ ---
       if interval == 6:
           cost += 20.0      # トライトーン跳躍: 禁止的
       elif interval == 3:
           prev_pc = prev_free % 12
           curr_pc = curr_free % 12
           if hasattr(self, '_key_scale'):
               sc = self._key_scale
           else:
               sc = set()
           if sc and (prev_pc not in sc or curr_pc not in sc):
               cost += 15.0  # 増2度: 禁止的
       ```
     - **`_score_transition` semitone clash penalty rewritten** — now checks all fixed voices for pc_diff==1 with cost +12.0, plus cross-chromatic penalty +6.0:
       ```python
       # --- 半音衝突ペナルティ ---
       curr_pc = curr_free % 12
       for name, melody in fixed_voices.items():
           if beat >= len(melody):
               continue
           fixed_pitch = melody[beat]
           if fixed_pitch is None:
               continue
           fixed_pc = fixed_pitch % 12
           pc_diff = min(abs(curr_pc - fixed_pc), 12 - abs(curr_pc - fixed_pc))
           if pc_diff == 1:
               cost += 12.0  # 半音衝突: 禁止的
       ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/vns_refiner.py`** (~700 lines)
     - **Semitone clash moved from L1 to L0** (fatal level, same priority as parallel 5ths):
       ```python
       # === (0c) 半音衝突: 同一サブビートで半音差の2音がある ===
       for sb_offset in range(SB):
           abs_sb = sb_start + sb_offset
           sounding = []
           for vt in active_voices:
               p = grid[vt][abs_sb]
               if p is not None:
                   sounding.append(p)
           for ii in range(len(sounding)):
               for jj in range(ii + 1, len(sounding)):
                   diff = abs(sounding[ii] - sounding[jj])
                   if diff == 1 or diff == 11:
                       pc_pair = {sounding[ii] % 12, sounding[jj] % 12}
                       leading = (key.tonic_pc - 1) % 12
                       if pc_pair == {leading, key.tonic_pc}:
                           continue
                       score.level0_fatal += 1
       ```
     - **Augmented intervals moved from L2 to L1**:
       ```python
       interval_mod = leap % 12
       if interval_mod == 3:
           prev_pc = prev_head % 12
           curr_pc = curr_head % 12
           if prev_pc not in key.scale or curr_pc not in key.scale:
               score.level1_harmony += 1  # 増2度
       elif interval_mod == 6:
           score.level1_harmony += 1       # トライトーン跳躍
       ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_quality_checker.py`**
     - **`_check_chromatic_clash` fixed** — was collecting all PCs within a beat per voice (including decoration notes from different subbeats), leading to false positives when same voice plays C→C# as decoration. Fixed to check only inter-voice clashes:
       ```python
       # 声部ごとのPC集合を構築(声部間の比較のため)
       voice_pcs: Dict[FugueVoiceType, Set[int]] = {}
       for vt, pitches in bp.items():
           voice_pcs[vt] = {p % 12 for p in pitches}
       # 異なる声部間で半音衝突をチェック
       vt_list = list(voice_pcs.keys())
       reported: Set[Tuple[int, int]] = set()
       for i in range(len(vt_list)):
           for j in range(i + 1, len(vt_list)):
               for pc_a in voice_pcs[vt_list[i]]:
                   for pc_b in voice_pcs[vt_list[j]]:
                       diff = (pc_b - pc_a) % 12
                       if diff == 1 or diff == 11:
                           pair = (min(pc_a, pc_b), max(pc_a, pc_b))
                           if pair in reported:
                               continue
                           if pc_a in diatonic and pc_b in diatonic:
                               continue
                           reported.add(pair)
                           # ... report violation
       ```

   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/generate_art_of_fugue.py`** — Generation script (unchanged this session)
   - **`/sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/fuge_final/src/fugue_structure.py`** — Contains `Key` class with `.scale` property

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **Edit tool duplicate match for coda VNS insertion**: Phase E MIDI output code was identical across sections. Fixed by including more surrounding context (the `sb_offset += dur` line before) to make the match unique.
   - **Checker false positives**: `_check_chromatic_clash` reported C vs C# when both occurred in the same beat in the SAME voice (decoration C→C#). VNS showed L0=0 but checker showed warnings. Root cause found by adding debug output to beat 17: alto had `C(60) | C(60) | C#(61) | C#(61)` — sequential, never simultaneous with soprano's A. Fixed by restructuring checker to only compare across different voices.
   - **DP penalties too weak**: `_score_vertical` minor 2nd cost was only +3.0, easily outweighed by chord completion bonus (-4.0 + -3.0). Fixed by raising to +15.0.
   - **No augmented interval penalty in DP**: `_score_transition` had no concept of augmented intervals. Added tritone +20.0 and aug2 +15.0.
   - **Key.scale bug discovered**: `Key(2, 'minor')` constructs with tonic_pc=0 (C), not 2 (D). Only `Key('D', 'minor')` works correctly. This means `self._key_scale = set(self.key.scale)` in the engine may use wrong scale depending on how Key was constructed. The generate script uses `Key('D', 'minor')` so it works, but the augmented interval detection in `_score_transition` that checks `self._key_scale` could be affected.
   - **User feedback on approach**:
     - "増音程イコール不協和音ではないですよ" — augmented intervals aren't dissonance per se, they sound like foreign keys
     - "展開型を変えて回避するのが普通では?" — changing voicing/inversion is the standard approach, not penalty tuning
     - "増音程を単純に禁止して仕舞えば、それ以外の組み合わせが必然的に選ばれる" — just prohibit them; alternatives will be chosen
     - "守るべきはまず禁止事項と命令事項です" — priorities: prohibitions and imperatives first, then recommendations

5. Problem Solving:
   - **SOLVED**: VNS applied to all sections (exposition + episodes + middle entries + coda)
   - **SOLVED**: DP semitone clash at beat level (4→0 at DP stage)
   - **SOLVED**: Checker false positives for intra-voice chromatic motion
   - **SOLVED**: VNS semitone clash priority (moved to L0 fatal)
   - **PARTIALLY SOLVED**: Augmented intervals reduced but 21 remain in final output, 13 at DP level
   - **IDENTIFIED BUT NOT YET FIXED**: Root cause of remaining augmented intervals is **voice leading / voicing choice**, not penalty magnitude. Gm→A with same inversion forces Bb→C# (aug2); changing inversion avoids it.
   - **IDENTIFIED BUT NOT YET FIXED**: Key.scale bug — `Key(integer, mode)` doesn't set tonic_pc correctly
   - **Current state**: errors=6, warnings=36 (from initial errors=7, warnings=64)
     - errors: 6 parallel 5ths/8ves in episodes/middle entries
     - warnings: 15 semitone clashes (mostly modulating sections, subject-driven) + 21 augmented intervals

6. All user messages:
   - "フォールバックをする仕組みがありながら、なぜこれだけ不協和音の嵐なのでしょう。出力が得られませんでしたというのならわかりますが。" (Why so many dissonances despite having fallback? If it reported "no output" that would be understandable.)
   - "増音程イコール不協和音ではないですよ。不協和音というより、突然の他調のコードのように聞こえるから駄目なんでしょう。トライトーンは、属七にも、長音階にも含まれていますからね。避けられませんが、C#はフーガの5度上の主題で不可避だからといって無神経に鳴らせばいいわけではない。半音衝突も経過音ならまだしも、隣同士の短二度の衝突はMajor7thを展開系で使わない限りあり得ないし、経過音でも避けるべきでしょう。長二度ですら耳障りですから。" (Augmented intervals ≠ dissonance; they sound like sudden foreign keys. Tritones are in dominant 7ths. C# is unavoidable but shouldn't be careless. Semitone clashes should be avoided even as passing tones. Even major 2nds are harsh.)
   - "Bb-C#の問題はGm->Aの進行を同じ展開型で並べると起きる現象ですよね。展開型を変えて回避するのが普通では?" (The Bb-C# problem comes from using same inversion across Gm→A. Changing inversion is the normal solution, right?)
   - "私のポイントは、増音程を単純に禁止して仕舞えば、それ以外の組み合わせが必然的に選ばれるということです。計算速度を上げるためには、真っ先に和声学の推奨方法に従うのが賢明だと思いますが、守るべきはまず禁止事項と命令事項です。" (My point is: simply prohibit augmented intervals and other combinations will necessarily be chosen. For speed, follow textbook harmony, but priorities are prohibitions and imperatives first.)

7. Pending Tasks:
   - **Make augmented intervals a HARD prohibition** (not soft penalty) — user's most recent explicit request. Currently +15.0/+20.0 penalties but user says to simply prohibit them so alternatives are forced.
   - Fix the Key.scale bug (`Key(integer, mode)` sets wrong tonic_pc)
   - Potentially implement proper voice leading rules (voicing changes across chord progressions) as the fundamental solution to augmented intervals
   - Address remaining 6 errors (parallel 5ths/8ves in non-exposition sections)
   - Address remaining semitone clashes (15 warnings)

8. Current Work:
   The user's most recent message states: "私のポイントは、増音程を単純に禁止して仕舞えば、それ以外の組み合わせが必然的に選ばれるということです...守るべきはまず禁止事項と命令事項です。"
   
   This was immediately followed by the summary request, so no implementation was started for this. The user is directing that augmented intervals should be treated as **hard prohibitions** (candidates excluded or infinite penalty) rather than soft penalties that can be overridden by bonuses. The user's design philosophy: enforce prohibitions first, then apply recommended practices.

   The most recent code state has:
   - DP: augmented interval penalties at +15.0/+20.0 (soft, can still be chosen)
   - VNS: augmented intervals at L1 (harmony level, below L0 fatal)
   - Results: errors=6, warnings=36

9. Optional Next Step:
   Convert augmented interval handling from soft penalties to **hard prohibitions** in the DP candidate generation. Per the user's directive: "増音程を単純に禁止して仕舞えば、それ以外の組み合わせが必然的に選ばれる" — either exclude candidates that would create augmented intervals from the DP search space entirely, or use prohibitive cost (e.g., +infinity / +1000.0) that no combination of bonuses can override. Also fix the Key.scale bug which affects scale-dependent augmented interval detection.

If you need specific details from before compaction (like exact code snippets, error messages, or content you generated), read the full transcript at: /sessions/fervent-vigilant-hypatia/mnt/.claude/projects/-sessions-fervent-vigilant-hypatia/94fa0e52-d9c0-47af-8920-50e9f6a6d6c6.jsonl
Please continue the conversation from where we left off without asking the user any further questions. Continue with the last task that you were asked to work on.

### queue-operation

和声学では、一声の増音程進行を禁じていますが、和声においては増六度を含む和音を幅広く許容しています。加えて増四度は展開すれば減五度で和音ではごく当たり前の音程です。

### queue-operation

導音C#と自然7度Cの同時鳴響。これは和声的短音階と自然短音階の混在で、ある意味不可避、とありますが教科書ではどうするか記載はないのですか？

### queue-operation

主題で導音であるC#が現れる場所は和声学のセオリー的には属和音か属七、あるいはその代理和音です。具体的にはA/A7/C#dim....。その部分だけはDの和声的短音階（Bbのフラットが取れないで旋律的にはならない）を対旋律に用いるのが1080 Contrapunctus 1をざっとみたところです。この部分をDの自然的短音階を使うから必然的に衝突が起きるのでしょう。そういう基本的な選択の誤りがエラーの原因でしょう。

### queue-operation

常にコードとスケールのマッチングをチェックし、コード優先でスケールを合わせ込むべきでしょう。モード奏法じゃないのでスケール優先はあり得ません。選択するスケールもなるべくその部分の原調（転調を考慮する）に対して臨時記号が少なくかつ合理的な選択が必要です。ただしコードより優先されるのが主題です。今の例のようにコードは主題に従うべきです。

### queue-operation

### queue-operation

あのね。作曲家でも、あるところで解がなければ、少し前から別の組み合わせでやり直すのですよ。将棋と一緒。そうしなければ、本質的に不要なはずの新たな制約を書くことになるでしょう？最後に関門を設けてそこでダメなら問答無用でフォールバックすればにも問題ないでしょう。もし最初の一小節まで失敗するならアルゴリズムが決定的に間違っていると言うこと。作曲家は300年古典和声学で何不自由なくやってきたのだから。
